  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_2723c6eb-ec96-426c-abf8-35741c0a18be'
      });
    }

<div id="review_3454737969" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3454737969" />
    <a title="Book Reviewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/115088874-book-reviewer"><img alt="Book Reviewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1589311806p2/115088874.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3454737969?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Book Reviewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Book Reviewer" href="/user/show/115088874-book-reviewer">Book Reviewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3454737969" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8753588977579926142">Frankie the Ferret is a wonderful children's picture book that will help young readers learn what it is like to have a ferret as a pet. Readers get to see all of the different types of activities that ferrets enjoy. The story is told through beautiful narrative illustrations and simple rhymes that really bring this story, and Frankie, to life.<br/><br/>I have never had a ferret for a pet, so I found this book immensely helpful in understanding what to expect if I were to have a pet ferret. This could also</span>
  <span id="freeText8753588977579926142" style="display:none">Frankie the Ferret is a wonderful children's picture book that will help young readers learn what it is like to have a ferret as a pet. Readers get to see all of the different types of activities that ferrets enjoy. The story is told through beautiful narrative illustrations and simple rhymes that really bring this story, and Frankie, to life.<br /><br />I have never had a ferret for a pet, so I found this book immensely helpful in understanding what to expect if I were to have a pet ferret. This could also be helpful for children who are also thinking of having a ferret as a pet. It's a simple introduction to the life of a ferret and the different types of mischief he can get into. This is a creative story for new readers that will help build vocabulary skills as much of the text is depicted throughout he story and the rhymes are simple and effective.<br /><br />This is a fun and educational story that parents will love reading with their children. With plenty of charming images of Frankie in various states of play, readers will sure enjoy reading this book more than once, or just flipping through the pages to giggle at Frankie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8753588977579926142" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Great for families that love pets, and also for any family that has lost a pet. Lots of other animals too.</span>

<div id="review_3449541937" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3449541937" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3449541937?book_show_action=true">Jul 18, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3449541937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7332557963203269328">‘Have you ever seen me prance when I’m happy and I’m free?’<br/><br/>Canadian author Kimberly Paterson offers her debut children’s book – FRANKIE THE FERRET – a story that reflects her family life: ‘Frankie was our beloved pet for nine years and provided us with endless amusement with his funny little antics.’<br/><br/>Kimberly’s charming rhyming words are offered as she introduces the principle character – ‘Hi! I’m Frankie the Ferret. I have big brown eyes. I’m nothing like a parrot. I cannot fly through skies. I </span>
  <span id="freeText7332557963203269328" style="display:none">‘Have you ever seen me prance when I’m happy and I’m free?’<br /><br />Canadian author Kimberly Paterson offers her debut children’s book – FRANKIE THE FERRET – a story that reflects her family life: ‘Frankie was our beloved pet for nine years and provided us with endless amusement with his funny little antics.’<br /><br />Kimberly’s charming rhyming words are offered as she introduces the principle character – ‘Hi! I’m Frankie the Ferret. I have big brown eyes. I’m nothing like a parrot. I cannot fly through skies. I really love to play all night and (yawn) to sleep all day. Sometimes I like to pretend to fight, and I might nip while I play…’ And as we follow the antic of Frankie, we learn many of his traits, and in doing so not only learn to love Frankie but we also learn about this very special animal species – the ferret – as a pet. <br /><br />Since the excellent illustrations are not designated to an artist, we must assume the fine images are the work of Kimberly Paterson! This is a fun, entertaining and sensitive little book that teaches children about pets (and special ferrets in particular!) while celebrating the author’s own pet, Frankie. Recommended. </span>
  <a data-text-id="7332557963203269328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText10455370898507210649" style="display:none">I have a five-year-old niece who really loves books and is obsessed with animals of all shapes and sizes. We have read lots of stories about dogs, and her favourite animal, cats, so I was looking for a cute and cuddle animal was a little more unusual. That's when I found 'Frankie the Ferret' by Kimberley Patterson.<br /><br />It was such a charming story about a beloved pet that brought so much joy to his family and to me and my niece as we read it together. My two-year-old nephew also giggles along and pointed to the cute pictures as we read it. Now my niece wants a ferret for a pet, I don't blame her after reading about Frankie.<br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hOhFwXy0J0I3WjkcqvYRYaIVGBM8UXSDEDFCf5TB50Hr7KhAAL2A45TSQxfivm+TnyZrcHgC5SOJKG8cYFaXGg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XxOYjeX9eFvUftFCSw8SPzf1Vx4r+z4jg0TN02KTjyswF3UMmfTf+nf2q0kDR2zNCsYkfW+or4MaXeCwlgT/cA==')})
  }
